# Document Migration Evidence Ledger

## Overview

This durable ledger records one reviewed migration disposition for every target Markdown path in the post-ADM-002 inventory. It preserves the exact local evidence, format-source applicability, destination, freshness trigger, and reviewer boundary needed by the later ADM waves.

## Reference Type

- Type: repository migration evidence ledger
- Inventory date: 2026-07-14
- Inventory boundary: 489 current paths, including this ledger's pinned self-row
- Format-source basis: `document-type-format-and-evidence-contract.md` observed 2026-07-12

## Authority Boundary

This file is authoritative for reviewed migration dispositions and their evidence/freshness routing. It does not replace the source document, accepted ADR, provider specification, executable asset, active governance owner, live cluster evidence, or the later ADM wave's topic-level source review.

## Scope

The ledger covers the exact validator inventory. Cloud example sources are merged only after ADM-006's 59-path and inbound-link proof; accepted, completed, archived, dated, template, README, Claude-native, repository-local adapter/baseline, and protected surfaces retain their explicit preservation boundaries. Gemini CLI native `.gemini/**` remains absent and outside this inventory.

## Sources

- [Document Type Format and Evidence Contract](./document-type-format-and-evidence-contract.md) is the reviewed type-to-source matrix used for row-level format applicability.
- [Current research pack](./README.md) owns the dated topic-source boundaries and provider/model cutoff used by later review waves.
- Repository inventory evidence comes from `scripts/validate-links-and-owners.py --inventory --format json` and the approved baseline identity recorded by Spec 030.

## Review and Freshness

- ADM-006 current-inventory result: the first table contains exactly 427 current corpus rows; the separate history table retains exactly 59 source-deleted `merge` rows with their complete evidence, official-source, applicability, decision, refresh, reviewer, result, and destination fields.
- ADM-006 README handoff result: schema 2 records exactly 52 active current README paths and 20 retired baseline paths; the retired set is absent from the current corpus, is owned by `ADM-006`, and maps only to the provider-correct dated AWS (`10`) or Azure (`10`) snapshot destination.
- Review boundary: local path/profile/disposition evidence is reviewed now; topical technical claims are revalidated by the owning ADM wave before transformation or merge.
- Refresh trigger: each row's trigger, any inventory membership change, or any changed registry/profile/source authority.
